<Pictures>None</Pictures><review>To be honest, I am a little baffled how this spot could be rated "best of" anything. It's a  chipotle knockoff in most respects. The signage indicates being rated or voted the best of newark or whatever for a couple years.

The inside looks a bit run down. The walls have some Cali fan swag hanging on it I guess to match their name. The soda fountain is oddly placed right next to the register. Theres also some older house cabinetry circa 1995 near the back hallway leading to what I think was their restroom that I could smell from the cash register.

If you've had chipotle, you've had this. My burrito was no better or worse than any other I've had in places like these. The service was average and came from a couple younger aged workers just going through the daily motions.

What bugged me the most is they appear to have a fly problem. Saw more than a couple of those little ones that typically mill about unclean outdoor garbage cans inside. A few of them buzzed around my burrito as I was eating and had to shoo them away constantly.

They had a filthy trash can sitting just inside the entryway as well. I suppose so you could toss your garbage away quickly while trying to make a hasty getaway from this not so "best of" eatery.

Whoever voted this place as being the best needs to get out more.
If this is the best, I shudder to think what the worst would be.< /review><Date>1576203182485<//Date><Gmap_id>0x808fbf5444ecb953:0x995b4df09fed4e2b< /Gmap_id>< UserId.>

<Pictures>None</Pictures><Rating>5<//Rating><Date>1423200284473</Date><Name>Jen H</Name><userid>100366113117526980111< /userid><Review>Is it Cal eats Fresh Mexican Grill as in a guy/girl named Cal that eats it or is Cal like California eats Fresh Mexican Grill? who knows but if you go here, then you're the one eating fresh Mexican Grill.

5 Stars... better believe it! It was seriously that good. You walk in and you can smell the goodness and the you just know you're going to sit there in a food coma. I came here with my boyfriend and we ordered a cajun shrimp burrito, shrimp and steak bowl, and 2 blackened fish tacos. The servers/cooks there were really friendly and helpful, they helped my indecisive self decide what to get or else I would have been standing there an eternity before I could decide.

Fish Tacos: This was superb. The fish had so much flavor, the tortilla was soft but held the taco together, and the sauce and the toppings were fresh. If you're gonna get one thing here, then get this because like the guy at the counter said to me and boyfriend, " you're gonna want more, trust me." He was totally right.

Cajun Shrimp Burrito: Large pieces of shrimp and the burrito was filled with them, every bite had shrimp. The shrimp was also spicy! A little bit too oily for my liking but I really liked the flavor.

Shrimp and Steak Bowl: Thank you to the guy who told us to get in a bowl because it was really good in bowl form and I can't imagine it as a wrap, I feel like you would get less of the food stuff and more tortilla. The steak was the real star because it was bursting with flavor. I feel like this was the dish that showcased their mastery of the grill.

The prices were reasonable, their portions were great, and the service was wonderful. I hope they keep it up because they are an excellent choice if you're in the mood for fresh mexican grill!<//Review><resp>None</resp><gmap_id>0x808fbf5444ecb953:0x995b4df09fed4e2b<//gmap_id></record>

Before I begin I always wish best of everyone and I always have a passion for truth and justice. I‚Äôm also not xenophobic and I also passionately believe in a world of color, different cultures and faiths.
Whoever reads this review I want the reader to know that this is not just a review but a strong and urgent warning! What I‚Äôm about to write I do not take lightly, but only as a last resort to hopefully prevent someone from possible death.

About a couple of years ago, my fianc√© needed a hysterectomy because of cysts located on her ovary.
Dr. Roya Rhakashani was recommended by her primary care physician, who we later found out was a close friend. The procedure was considered routine and she would have been discharged that day.

For the sake of the reader, I‚Äôll try to be as brief as possible. After being reassured that everything went well, we found ourselves back in the emergency room where she was admitted for severe abdominal cavity infection. Exploratory surgery was performed where they discovered a cut in her bladder and a cut in her ureter tube.
Within a couple of days she went into septic shock and needed emergency surgery to flush out her cavity that severely infected. Later the Dr. confided in us how close to death she was and it was a last minute call to do the surgery that saved her life.
A catheter, two nephrostomy tubes to bypass the kidneys and for drains for her abdominal cavity were added.
Almost 3 months were spent in and out of the hospital to recover and about a year while still having 7 drain tubes attached to her body, was she finally able to have her reconstructive surgery. Fortunately for us the best reconstructive surgeon in the nation performed this surgery and it went well.
Being an engineer by trade, I asked one of the team of Dr.s at the hospital as to how do they prevent things like this happening in the future. I was greatly disappointed to learn that the Doctors would initiate an inquiry with Dr Rhakashani, to determine what went wrong and to see what can be done to prevent this in the future. The problem is that this inquiry was voluntary and if they did have one, nothing would go in record and whatever was discussed stayed with the doctors? Also; every single doctor that attend to my girlfriend confided in us there sympathy and anger with Dr. Rhakashani and even intimating that they were not surprised and that they have issues with her before.
Because of any lack of professional recourse we did look into legal recourse to one: hopefully to prevent this happening to someone else in the future and two: to have some competition for over a years worth of pain, both physical and emotional.
This the classic David vs. Goliath story where in this story Goliath wins by default, because David isn‚Äôt even allowed to have his day, only if David died, then he might have his day. In other words, Malpractice is severally slanted on the physicians side due to no changes to the malpractice laws since 1976. This is due to Insurance companies investing millions of dollars to fight any bill that would be introduced to update these laws. Why, because it literally saves them millions, if not billions in paying out even fair settlements. One attorney said that the best case is if the person died from gross negligence and even then there is max payout of only $250,000.0 and that‚Äôs in the law! Also; one attorney told me that he had tried a case against Dr. Rhakashani a few years ago. Also; during my girlfriends recovery one of her doctors office assistants also had an issue 7 years earlier when performing an emergency C- section she cut her infant daughters scalp which she has a long scar acids her forehead today.
Also; Another attorney flat out told us that her husband was a prominent attorney and he did not want to suffer and retribution to himself and carrier if he took the case.
So please head these words and if you still wish to use her, just know that there is virtually no recourse for you.<//Review>

Training Portion: This center is not out to make a quick buck by selling anything and everything to you. Student rate discounts on gear and rental equipment are a godsend. I had an outdated book and Rick offered to let me borrow a current version for free rather than have me buy a new student package. From being a little n00b tadpole in the confines of pool dives to spreading my fins and gliding at the bottom of the restless pacific for the open water portion I never once felt in danger with this cadre of well trained instructors. Steve was very patient with my girlfriend while she tried on Tons of masks and he explained pros and cons of each mask and style. Now my girlfriend already knew what fins she wanted from our searching online, she wanted the ones hat looked like Mermaid fins, yeah I know palm to forehead. We did not see them on the display shelf and asked Steve about them and he said they were in the warehouse for online sales and asked if we could give him a min to send a runner to get them for us! While we waited for the runner we asked about wetsuits and Steve once again was very patient with her as she tried in a few sizes and styles. Steve explained each style in very great detail and gave recommendations on what ones he thinks would fit her and meet her needs but did Not steer her into any one brand and did not try to Upsale a more expensive suit. Now we did not plan on getting a wetsuit at this time and we told Steve this but that did not deter him from giving us tons of knowledge and advice on what to look for when we were ready to get one and he Never pressured her to make a purchase. The runner came back with several sizes of fins in the color and style we wanted but when Steve had her try them on he realized she needed the size in between the two, of which the runner was unable to find. Steve did not simply accept this and try to sell us a different fin, no he went to the warehouse himself and eventually found her size and color!
Now we are checking out with her fins, mask and snorkel and Steve shows us the deal we got for doing a bundle and the discount for being students. Wow! We ask if he could show us what it would cost if we got the wetsuit today... again wow! Just to give you an idea, and this will very depending on how much you bundle and on Brand specific packages but we got a mask that was $120 for $79 and a wetsuit that was $400 for $319. That‚Äôs just some of huge savings Steve was able to get. After seeing this we decided to get Everthing including a BCD+Regulator package and the more we got the more we saved! After getting all this gear Steve went to Michael Johnson (the owner) and he took care of us even More! My girlfriend now has Everything she needs to scuba dive and the best part is she will get to learn from the very begginging on Her Own gear and build that confidence with it right away! Thank you so much to Steve Gilmore and Michael Johnson and the rest of the crew at Dolphin Scuba!!< /text>
